The FK relationships that can cause this are:\n\n1. **CareProfile GĺĆ Taxonomy**: `Taxonomy.CareProfileId` references `CareProfile`\n2. **Taxonomy GĺĆ Plant/SeedBatch**: `InventoryItem.TaxonomyId` references `Taxonomy`\n3. **Plant/SeedBatch GĺĆ Lineage**: `Lineage.MotherId` / `Lineage.FatherId` references InventoryItem with `OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict)`\n\n### Solution design\n\n**Repository layer**: Add a dependency check inside each `Delete` method. If dependents exist, throw `InvalidOperationException` with a friendly message.\n\n**Controller layer**: Wrap the `_repository.Delete(id)` call in a `try-catch (InvalidOperationException)`. On catch: set `TempData["DeleteError"]` and redirect to `Details` (with the id). On success: redirect to `Index` as now.\n\n**View layer**: Add a TempData error display to each of the 4 Details views, just above the action-panel.\n\n---\n\n### 1. `Repositories/CareProfileRepository.cs`\n\nIn the `Delete` method, add a check BEFORE `_db.CareProfile.Remove(entity)`:\n\n```csharp\npublic void Delete(int id)\n{\n var entity = _db.CareProfile.Find(id);\n if (entity != null)\n {\n bool hasReferences = _db.Taxonomy.Any(t => t.CareProfileId == id);\n if (hasReferences)\n throw new InvalidOperationException(\n "This care profile cannot be deleted because one or more taxonomies are assigned to it. Remove or reassign those taxonomies first.");\n\n _db.CareProfile.Remove(entity);\n _db.SaveChanges();\n }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 2. `Repositories/TaxonomyRepository.cs`\n\nIn the `Delete` method, add a check before removing:\n\n```csharp\npublic void Delete(int id)\n{\n var entity = _db.Taxonomy.Find(id);\n if (entity != null)\n {\n bool hasPlants = _db.Plant.Any(p => p.TaxonomyId == id);\n bool hasSeedBatches = _db.SeedBatch.Any(s => s.TaxonomyId == id);\n if (hasPlants || hasSeedBatches)\n throw new InvalidOperationException(\n "This taxonomy cannot be deleted because plants or seed batches are assigned to it. Remove or reassign those records first.");\n\n _db.Taxonomy.Remove(entity);\n _db.SaveChanges();\n }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 3. `Repositories/PlantRepository.cs`\n\nIn the `Delete` method, add a check before removing:\n\n```csharp\npublic void Delete(int id)\n{\n var entity = _db.Plant.Find(id);\n if (entity != null)\n {\n bool usedInLineage = _db.Lineage.Any(l => l.MotherId == id || l.FatherId == id);\n if (usedInLineage)\n throw new InvalidOperationException(\n "This plant cannot be deleted because it is recorded as a parent in one or more lineage entries. Remove those lineage records first.");\n\n _db.Plant.Remove(entity);\n _db.SaveChanges();\n }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 4. `Repositories/SeedBatchRepository.cs`\n\nIn the `Delete` method, add a check before removing:\n\n```csharp\npublic void Delete(int id)\n{\n var entity = _db.SeedBatch.Find(id);\n if (entity != null)\n {\n bool usedInLineage = _db.Lineage.Any(l => l.MotherId == id || l.FatherId == id);\n if (usedInLineage)\n throw new InvalidOperationException(\n "This seed batch cannot be deleted because it is recorded as a parent in one or more lineage entries. Remove those lineage records first.");\n\n _db.SeedBatch.Remove(entity);\n _db.SaveChanges();\n }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 5. `Controllers/CareProfileController.cs`\n\nChange the `Delete` action from:\n```csharp\n [HttpPost]\n [Route("delete/{id:int}")]\n [ValidateAntiForgeryToken]\n public IActionResult Delete(int id)\n {\n if (!IsAdmin) return RequireAdmin();\n _careProfileRepository.Delete(id);\n return RedirectToAction("Index");\n }\n```\n\nTo:\n```csharp\n [HttpPost]\n [Route("delete/{id:int}")]\n [ValidateAntiForgeryToken]\n public IActionResult Delete(int id)\n {\n if (!IsAdmin) return RequireAdmin();\n try\n {\n _careProfileRepository.Delete(id);\n return RedirectToAction("Index");\n }\n catch (InvalidOperationException ex)\n {\n TempData["DeleteError"] = ex.Message;\n return RedirectToAction("Details", new { id });\n }\n }\n```\n\n---\n\n### 6. `Controllers/TaxonomyController.cs`\n\nSame pattern.
